  <div style="margin-left:7.731%;text-indent:0;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:6.667%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:7.225612069058946%;">3.8</font><div style="display:inline;" id="x_8_quorum_1"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Quorum</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">.</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.35pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:6pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="margin-left:1.107%;text-indent:6.814%;font-size:10pt;margin-top:4.55pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;margin-right:1.056%;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">At all meetings of the Board, unless otherwise provided by the Certificate of Incorporation, a majority of the total number of directors shall constitute a quorum for the transaction of business. The vote of a majority of the directors present at any meeting at which a quorum is present shall be the act of the Board, except as may be otherwise specifically provided by statute, the Certificate of Incorporation or these bylaws. If a quorum is not present at any meeting of the Board, then the directors present thereat may adjourn the meeting from time to time, without notice other than announcement at the meeting, until a quorum is present.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="margin-left:0.56%;text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.55pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:center;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">14</font></p>
  <hr style="page-break-after:always;">
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:7.731%;text-indent:0;display:flex;margin-top:4.6pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:6.667%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:7.225612069058946%;">3.9</font><div style="display:inline;" id="x_9_board_action_without_a_meeting"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Board Action without a Meeting</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">.</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.45pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:6pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="margin-left:1.107%;text-indent:6.814%;font-size:10pt;margin-top:4.6pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;margin-right:1.056%;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Unless otherwise restricted by the Certificate of Incorporation or these bylaws, any action required or permitted to be taken at any meeting of the Board, or of any committee thereof, may be taken without a meeting if all members of the Board or committee, as the case may be, consent thereto in writing or by electronic transmission. After an action is taken, the consent or consents relating thereto shall be filed with the minutes of the proceedings of the Board, or the committee thereof, in the same paper or electronic form as the minutes are maintained. Such action by written consent or consent by electronic transmission shall have the same force and effect as a unanimous vote of the Board.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.05pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10.5pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:7.731%;text-indent:0;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:6.667%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:7.225612069058946%;">3.10</font><div style="display:inline;" id="x_10_fees_and_compensation_of_directors"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Fees and Compensation of Directors</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">.</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.35pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:6pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="margin-left:1.107%;text-indent:6.815%;font-size:10pt;margin-top:4.6pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;margin-right:1.074%;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Unless otherwise restricted by the Certificate of Incorporation or these bylaws, the Board shall have the authority to fix the compensation, including fees and reimbursement of expenses, of directors for services to the Corporation in any capacity.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="margin-left:26.16%;text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:9.75pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;margin-right:26.157%;text-align:center;" id="article_iv____committees"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Article IV - Committees</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.15pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10.5pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:7.731%;text-indent:0;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:6.667%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:7.225612069058946%;">4.1</font><div style="display:inline;" id="x_1_committees_of_directors"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Committees of Directors</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">.</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.35pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:6pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="margin-left:1.107%;text-indent:6.812%;font-size:10pt;margin-top:4.6pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;margin-right:1.028%;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">The Board may designate one (1) or more committees, each committee to consist, of one (1) or more of the directors of the Corporation. The Board may designate one (1) or more directors as alternate members of any committee, who may replace any absent or disqualified member at any meeting of the committee. In the absence or disqualification of a member of a committee, the member or members thereof present at any meeting and not disqualified from voting, whether or not such member or members constitute a quorum, may unanimously appoint another member of the Board to act at the meeting in the place of any such absent or disqualified member. Any such committee, to the extent provided in the resolution of the Board or in these bylaws, shall have and may exercise all the powers and authority of the Board in the management of the business and affairs of the Corporation, and may authorize the seal of the Corporation to be affixed to all papers that may require it; but no such committee shall have the power or authority to (i) approve or adopt, or recommend to the stockholders, any action or matter expressly required by the DGCL to be submitted to stockholders for approval, or (ii) adopt, amend or repeal any bylaw of the Corporation.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.05pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10.5pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:7.731%;text-indent:0;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:6.667%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:7.225612069058946%;">4.2</font><div style="display:inline;" id="x_2_committee_minutes"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Committee Minutes</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">.</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.35pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:6pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="margin-left:1.107%;text-indent:6.741%;font-size:10pt;margin-top:4.55pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Each committee shall keep regular minutes of its meetings and report the same to the Board when required.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.15pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:7.731%;text-indent:0;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:6.667%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:7.225612069058946%;">4.3</font><div style="display:inline;" id="x_3_meetings_and_actions_of_committees"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Meetings and Actions of Committees</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">.</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.5pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:6pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="margin-left:1.107%;text-indent:6.741%;font-size:10pt;margin-top:4.55pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Meetings and actions of committees shall be governed by, and held and taken in accordance with, the provisions of:</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.4pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:15.065%;text-indent:0;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:6%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:7.064225584270323%;">(i)</font><div style="display:inline;" id="xi__section_3_5__place_of_meetings__meet"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Section 3.5 (place of meetings; meetings by telephone);</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10.5pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:14.528%;text-indent:0;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:6.537%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:7.64811868214152%;">(ii)</font><div style="display:inline;" id="xii__section_3_6__regular_meetings__"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Section 3.6 (regular meetings);</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="margin-left:0.56%;text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.55pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:center;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">15</font></p>
  <hr style="page-break-after:always;">
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:14%;text-indent:0;display:flex;margin-top:4.55pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:7.065%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:8.215116279069768%;">(iii)</font><div style="display:inline;" id="xiii__section_3_7__special_meetings__not"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Section 3.7 (special meetings; notice);</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10.5pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:14.13%;text-indent:0;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:6.935%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:8.076161639687898%;">(iv)</font><div style="display:inline;" id="xiv__section_3_9__board_action_without_a"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Section 3.9 (board action without a meeting); and</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.45pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:14.667%;text-indent:0;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:6.398%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:7.4976855378341325%;">(v)</font><div style="display:inline;" id="xv__section_7_13__waiver_of_notice__"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Section 7.13 (waiver of notice),</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10.5pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="margin-left:1.107%;text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">with such changes in the context of those bylaws as are necessary to substitute the committee and its members for the Board and its members. </font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">However</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">:</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.4pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:1.065%;text-indent:13.477%;font-size:0;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;margin-bottom:0;margin-right:1.065%;min-width:13.333%;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:3.775205943296103%;">(i)</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">the time of regular meetings of committees may be determined either by resolution of the Board or by resolution of the committee;</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.5pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:1.065%;text-indent:13.477%;font-size:0;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;margin-bottom:0;margin-right:1.065%;min-width:13.333%;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:3.775205943296103%;">(ii)</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">special meetings of committees may also be called by resolution of the Board or the chairperson of the applicable committee; and</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.55pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:1.065%;text-indent:13.477%;font-size:0;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;margin-bottom:0;margin-right:1.065%;min-width:13.333%;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:3.775205943296103%;">(iii)</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">the Board may adopt rules for the governance of any committee to override the provisions that would otherwise apply to the committee pursuant to this Section 4.3, provided that such rules do not violate the provisions of the Certificate of Incorporation or applicable law.</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.5pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:7.731%;text-indent:0;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:6.667%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:7.225612069058946%;">4.4</font><div style="display:inline;" id="x_4_subcommittees_"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Subcommittees.</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:6.5pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="margin-left:1.107%;text-indent:6.814%;font-size:10pt;margin-top:4.6pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;margin-right:1.056%;text-align:justify;" id="article_v____officers"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Unless otherwise provided in the Certificate of Incorporation, these bylaws or the resolutions of the Board designating the committee, a committee may create one (1) or more subcommittees, each subcommittee to consist of one (1) or more members of the committee, and delegate to a subcommittee any or all of the powers </font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">and authority of the committee.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="margin-left:26.16%;text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:10.1pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;margin-right:26.157%;text-align:center;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Article V - Officers</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.1pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10.5pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:7.731%;text-indent:0;display:flex;margin-top:0.05pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:6.667%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:7.225612069058946%;">5.1</font><div style="display:inline;" id="x_1_officers"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Officers</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">.</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.35pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:6pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="margin-left:1.107%;text-indent:6.815%;font-size:10pt;margin-top:4.55pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;margin-right:1.065%;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">The officers of the Corporation shall include a Chief Executive Officer, Chief Operating Officer, Chief Financial Officer, a President and a Secretary. The Corporation may also have, at the discretion of the Board, a Chairperson of the Board, a Vice Chairperson of the Board, a Chief Financial Officer, a Treasurer, one (1) or more Vice Presidents, one (1) or more Assistant Vice Presidents, one (1) or more Assistant Treasurers, one (1) or more Assistant Secretaries, and any such other officers as may be appointed in accordance with the provisions of these bylaws. Any number of offices may be held by the same person. No officer need be a stockholder or director of the Corporation.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.05pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10.5pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:7.731%;text-indent:0;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:6.667%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:7.225612069058946%;">5.2</font><div style="display:inline;" id="x_2_appointment_of_officers"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Appointment of Officers</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">.</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.35pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:6pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="margin-left:1.107%;text-indent:6.741%;font-size:10pt;margin-top:4.6pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">The Board shall appoint the officers of the Corporation, except such officers as may be appointed in accordance with the provisions of Section 5.3 of these bylaws.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.15pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:7.731%;text-indent:0;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:6.667%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:7.225612069058946%;">5.3</font><div style="display:inline;" id="x_3_subordinate_officers"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Subordinate Officers</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">.</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.45pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:6pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="margin-left:1.107%;text-indent:6.741%;font-size:10pt;margin-top:4.6pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">The Board may appoint, or empower the Chief Executive Officer or, in the absence of a Chief Executive Officer, the President, to appoint, such other officers and agents as the business of the Corporation may require.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="margin-left:0.56%;text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.55pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:center;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">16</font></p>
  <hr style="page-break-after:always;">
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="margin-left:1.107%;text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:4.55pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Each of such officers and agents shall hold office for such period, have such authority, and perform such duties as are provided in these bylaws or as the Board may from time to time determine.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.15pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:7.731%;text-indent:0;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:6.667%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:7.225612069058946%;">5.4</font><div style="display:inline;" id="x_4_removal_and_resignation_of_officers"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Removal and Resignation of Officers</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">.</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.5pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:6pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="margin-left:1.107%;text-indent:6.815%;font-size:10pt;margin-top:4.55pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;margin-right:1.074%;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Subject to the rights, if any, of an officer under any contract of employment, any officer may be removed, either with or without cause, by the Board or, except in the case of an officer chosen by the Board, by any officer upon whom such power of removal may be conferred by the Board.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.45pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="margin-left:1.107%;text-indent:6.815%;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;margin-right:1.074%;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Any officer may resign at any time by giving written notice to the Corporation. Any resignation shall take effect at the date of the receipt of that notice or at any later time specified in that notice. Unless otherwise specified in the notice of resignation, the acceptance of the resignation shall not be necessary to make it effective. Any resignation is without prejudice to the rights, if any, of the Corporation under any contract to which the officer is a party.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.05pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10.5pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:7.731%;text-indent:0;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:6.667%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:7.225612069058946%;">5.5</font><div style="display:inline;" id="x_5_vacancies_in_offices"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Vacancies in Offices</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">.</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.35pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:6pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="margin-left:1.107%;text-indent:6.741%;font-size:10pt;margin-top:4.6pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Any vacancy occurring in any office of the Corporation shall be filled by the Board or as provided in Section 5.2.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.15pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:7.731%;text-indent:0;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:6.667%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:7.225612069058946%;">5.6</font><div style="display:inline;" id="x_6_representation_of_shares_of_other_co"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Representation of Shares of Other Corporations</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">.</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.45pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:6pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="margin-left:1.107%;text-indent:6.815%;font-size:10pt;margin-top:4.6pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;margin-right:1.065%;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">The Chairperson of the Board, the Chief Executive Officer, or the President of this Corporation, or any other person authorized by the Board, the Chief Executive Officer or the President, is authorized to vote, represent and exercise on behalf of this Corporation all rights incident to any and all shares or voting securities of any other corporation or other person standing in the name of this Corporation. The authority granted herein may be exercised either by such person directly or by any other person authorized to do so by proxy or power of attorney duly executed by such person having the authority.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.55pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:7.731%;text-indent:0;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:6.667%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:7.225612069058946%;">5.7</font><div style="display:inline;" id="x_7_authority_and_duties_of_officers"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Authority and Duties of Officers</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">.</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.35pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:6pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="margin-left:1.107%;text-indent:6.815%;font-size:10pt;margin-top:4.6pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;margin-right:1.074%;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">All officers of the Corporation shall respectively have such authority and perform such duties in the management of the business of the Corporation as may be provided herein or designated from time to time by the Board and, to the extent not so provided, as generally pertain to their respective offices, subject to the control of the Board.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:7.731%;text-indent:0;display:flex;margin-top:0.05pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:6.667%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:7.225612069058946%;">5.8</font><div style="display:inline;" id="x_8_compensation_"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Compensation.</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.45pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:6pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="margin-left:1.107%;text-indent:6.815%;font-size:10pt;margin-top:4.6pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;margin-right:1.065%;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">The compensation of the officers of the Corporation for their services as such shall be fixed from time to time by or at the direction of the Board. An officer of the Corporation shall not be prevented from receiving compensation by reason of the fact that he or she is also a director of the Corporation.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="margin-left:26.16%;text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:10.25pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;margin-right:26.157%;text-align:center;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Article VI - Records</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.45pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="margin-left:1.107%;text-indent:6.814%;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;margin-right:1.056%;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">A stock ledger consisting of one or more records in which the names of all of the Corporation&#x2019;s stockholders of record, the address and number of shares registered in the name of each such stockholder, and all issuances and transfers of stock of the corporation are recorded in accordance with Section 224 of the DGCL</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="margin-left:0.56%;text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.55pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:center;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">17</font></p>
  <hr style="page-break-after:always;">
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="margin-left:1.107%;text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:4.55pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;margin-right:1.046%;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">shall be administered by or on behalf of the Corporation. Any records administered by or on behalf of the Corporation in the regular course of its business, including its stock ledger, books of account, and minute books, may be kept on, or by means of, or be in the form of, any information storage device, or method, or one or more electronic networks or databases (including one or more distributed electronic networks or databases), provided that the records so kept can be converted into clearly legible paper form within a reasonable time and, with respect to the stock ledger, that the records so kept (i) can be used to prepare the list of stockholders specified in Sections 219 and 220 of the DGCL, (ii) record the information specified in Sections 156, 159, 217(a) and 218 of the DGCL, and (iii) record transfers of stock as governed by Article 8 of the Uniform Commercial Code as adopted in the State of Delaware.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="margin-left:26.173%;text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:10.25pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;margin-right:26.157%;text-align:center;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Article VII - General Matters</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10.5pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:7.731%;text-indent:0;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:6.667%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:7.225612069058946%;">7.1</font><div style="display:inline;" id="x_1_execution_of_corporate_contracts_and"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Execution of Corporate Contracts and Instruments</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">.</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.5pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:6pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="margin-left:1.107%;text-indent:6.814%;font-size:10pt;margin-top:4.55pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;margin-right:1.056%;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">The Board, except as otherwise provided in these bylaws, may authorize any officer or officers, or agent or agents, to enter into any contract or execute any instrument in the name of and on behalf of the Corporation; such authority may be general or confined to specific instances.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.2pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:7.731%;text-indent:0;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:6.667%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:7.225612069058946%;">7.2</font><div style="display:inline;" id="x_2_stock_certificates"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Stock Certificates</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">.</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.5pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:6pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="margin-left:1.107%;text-indent:6.813%;font-size:10pt;margin-top:4.55pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;margin-right:1.037%;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">The shares of the Corporation shall be represented by certificates, provided that the Board by resolution may provide that some or all of the shares of any class or series of stock of the Corporation shall be uncertificated. Certificates for the shares of stock, if any, shall be in such form as is consistent with the Certificate of Incorporation and applicable law</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:10pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">. </font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Every holder of stock represented by a certificate shall be entitled to have a certificate signed by, or in the name of the Corporation by, any two officers authorized to sign stock certificates representing the number of shares registered in certificate form. The Chairperson or Vice Chairperson of the Board, Chief Executive Officer, the President, Vice President, the Treasurer, any Assistant Treasurer, the Secretary or any Assistant Secretary of the Corporation shall be specifically authorized to sign stock certificates. Any or all of the signatures on the certificate may be a facsimile. In case any officer, transfer agent or registrar who has signed or whose facsimile signature has been placed upon a certificate has ceased to be such officer, transfer agent or registrar before such certificate is issued, it may be issued by the Corporation with the same effect as if he or she were such officer, transfer agent or registrar at the date of issue.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.4pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="margin-left:1.107%;text-indent:6.815%;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;margin-right:1.065%;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">The Corporation may issue the whole or any part of its shares as partly paid and subject to call for the remainder of the consideration to be paid therefor. Upon the face or back of each stock certificate issued to represent any such partly paid shares, or upon the books and records of the Corporation in the case of uncertificated partly paid shares, the total amount of the consideration to be paid therefor and the amount paid thereon shall be stated. Upon the declaration of any dividend on fully paid shares, the Corporation shall declare a dividend upon partly paid shares of the same class, but only upon the basis of the percentage of the consideration actually paid thereon.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.55pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:7.731%;text-indent:0;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:6.667%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:7.225612069058946%;">7.3</font><div style="display:inline;" id="x_3_special_designation_of_certificates_"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Special Designation of Certificates.</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:6.5pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="margin-left:1.107%;text-indent:6.814%;font-size:10pt;margin-top:4.6pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;margin-right:1.056%;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">If the Corporation is authorized to issue more than one class of stock or more than one series of any class, then the powers, the designations, the preferences and the relative, participating, optional or other special rights of each class of stock or series thereof and the qualifications, limitations or restrictions of such preferences and/or rights shall be set forth in full or summarized on the face or on the back of the certificate that the</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="margin-left:0.56%;text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.55pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:center;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">18</font></p>
  <hr style="page-break-after:always;">
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="margin-left:1.107%;text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:4.55pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;margin-right:1.056%;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Corporation shall issue to represent such class or series of stock (or, in the case of uncertificated shares, set forth in a notice provided pursuant to Section 151 of the DGCL); provided, however, that except as otherwise provided in Section 202 of the DGCL, in lieu of the foregoing requirements, there may be set forth on the face of back of the certificate that the Corporation shall issue to represent such class or series of stock (or, in the case of any uncertificated shares, included in the aforementioned notice) a statement that the Corporation will furnish without charge to each stockholder who so requests the powers, the designations, the preferences and the relative, participating, optional or other special rights of each class of stock or series thereof and the qualifications, limitations or restrictions of such preferences and/or rights.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.15pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10.5pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:7.731%;text-indent:0;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:6.667%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:7.225612069058946%;">7.4</font><div style="display:inline;" id="x_4_lost_certificates"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Lost Certificates</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">.</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.35pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:6pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="margin-left:1.107%;text-indent:6.813%;font-size:10pt;margin-top:4.6pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;margin-right:1.037%;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Except as provided in this Section 7.4, no new certificates for shares shall be issued to replace a previously issued certificate unless the latter is surrendered to the Corporation and cancelled at the same time. The Corporation may issue a new certificate of stock or uncertificated shares in the place of any certificate theretofore issued by it, alleged to have been lost, stolen or destroyed, and the Corporation may require the owner of the lost, stolen or destroyed certificate, or such owner&#x2019;s legal representative, to give the Corporation a bond sufficient to indemnify it against any claim that may be made against it on account of the alleged loss, theft or destruction of any such certificate or the issuance of such new certificate or uncertificated shares.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.05pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10.5pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:7.731%;text-indent:0;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:6.667%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:7.225612069058946%;">7.5</font><div style="display:inline;" id="x_5_shares_without_certificates"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Shares Without Certificates</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.35pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:6pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="margin-left:1.107%;text-indent:6.814%;font-size:10pt;margin-top:4.6pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;margin-right:1.056%;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">The Corporation may adopt a system of issuance, recordation and transfer of its shares of stock by electronic or other means not involving the issuance of certificates, provided the use of such system by the Corporation is permitted in accordance with applicable law.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.1pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10.5pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:7.731%;text-indent:0;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:6.667%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:7.225612069058946%;">7.6</font><div style="display:inline;" id="x_6_construction__definitions"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Construction; Definitions</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">.</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.35pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:6pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="margin-left:1.107%;text-indent:6.813%;font-size:10pt;margin-top:4.6pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;margin-right:1.046%;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Unless the context requires otherwise, the general provisions, rules of construction and definitions in the DGCL shall govern the construction of these bylaws. Without limiting the generality of this provision, the singular number includes the plural and the plural number includes the singular.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.2pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:7.731%;text-indent:0;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:6.667%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:7.225612069058946%;">7.7</font><div style="display:inline;" id="x_7_dividends"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Dividends</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">.</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.5pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:6pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="margin-left:1.107%;text-indent:6.815%;font-size:10pt;margin-top:4.55pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;margin-right:1.065%;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">The Board, subject to any restrictions contained in either (i) the DGCL or (ii) the Certificate of Incorporation, may declare and pay dividends upon the shares of its capital stock. Dividends may be paid in cash, in property or in shares of the Corporation&#x2019;s capital stock.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.45pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="margin-left:1.107%;text-indent:6.815%;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.05pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;margin-right:1.065%;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">The Board may set apart out of any of the funds of the Corporation available for dividends a reserve or reserves for any proper purpose and may abolish any such reserve. Such purposes shall include but not be limited to equalizing dividends, repairing or maintaining any property of the Corporation, and meeting contingencies.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.55pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:7.731%;text-indent:0;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:6.667%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:7.225612069058946%;">7.8</font><div style="display:inline;" id="x_8_fiscal_year"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Fiscal Year</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">.</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.45pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:6pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="margin-left:7.773%;text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:4.6pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">The fiscal year of the Corporation shall be fixed by resolution of the Board and may be changed by the</font></p>
  <p style="margin-left:1.107%;text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.05pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Board.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="margin-left:0.56%;text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.55pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:center;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">19</font></p>
  <hr style="page-break-after:always;">
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:7.731%;text-indent:0;display:flex;margin-top:4.6pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:6.667%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:7.225612069058946%;">7.9</font><div style="display:inline;" id="x_9_seal"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Seal</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">.</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.45pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:6pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="margin-left:1.107%;text-indent:6.815%;font-size:10pt;margin-top:4.6pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;margin-right:1.074%;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">The Corporation may adopt a corporate seal, which shall be adopted and which may be altered by the Board. The Corporation may use the corporate seal by causing it or a facsimile thereof to be impressed or affixed or in any other manner reproduced.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.2pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:7.731%;text-indent:0;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:6.667%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:7.225612069058946%;">7.10</font><div style="display:inline;" id="x_10_transfer_of_stock"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Transfer of Stock</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">.</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.35pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:6pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="margin-left:1.107%;text-indent:6.813%;font-size:10pt;margin-top:4.6pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;margin-right:1.046%;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Shares of the Corporation shall be transferable in the manner prescribed by law and in these bylaws. Shares of stock of the Corporation shall be transferred on the books of the Corporation only by the holder of record thereof or by such holder&#x2019;s attorney duly authorized in writing, upon surrender to the Corporation of the certificate or certificates representing such shares endorsed by the appropriate person or persons (or by delivery of duly executed instructions with respect to uncertificated shares), with such evidence of the authenticity of such endorsement or execution, transfer, authorization and other matters as the Corporation may reasonably require, and accompanied by all necessary stock transfer stamps. No transfer of stock shall be valid as against the Corporation for any purpose until it shall have been entered in the stock records of the Corporation by an entry showing the names of the persons from and to whom it was transferred.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.05pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10.5pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:7.731%;text-indent:0;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:6.667%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:7.225612069058946%;">7.11</font><div style="display:inline;" id="x_11_stock_transfer_agreements"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Stock Transfer Agreements</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">.</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.5pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:6pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="margin-left:1.107%;text-indent:6.813%;font-size:10pt;margin-top:4.55pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;margin-right:1.046%;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">The Corporation shall have power to enter into and perform any agreement with any number of stockholders of any one or more classes or series of stock of the Corporation to restrict the transfer of shares of stock of the Corporation of any one or more classes owned by such stockholders in any manner not prohibited by the DGCL.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10.5pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:7.731%;text-indent:0;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:6.667%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:7.225612069058946%;">7.12</font><div style="display:inline;" id="x_12_registered_stockholders"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">Registered Stockholders</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">.</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:6.5pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="margin-left:7.773%;text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:4.6pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">The Corporation:</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0.3pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
